But corruption, legal loopholes, delays, and stretched resources combine to make the quest to jail the group far from straightforward.", "poster_path": "/uOVsNtECSWbRFgYw1Nzb9Bxy7zs.jpg", "media_type": "tv", "adult": false, "original_language": "en", "genre_ids": [18, 80], "popularity": 4.9233, "first_air_date": "1994-09-01", "vote_average": 9.0, "vote_count": 1, "origin_country": ["AU"]}]}]}
